    PROCEDURE MakeExcelInfo@3();
    BEGIN
      //ExcelBuf.SetUseInfoSheed;
        // Message('hi..');
      ExcelBuf.SetUseInfoSheet;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text005),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(COMPANYNAME,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text007),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text001),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text006),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(REPORT::"Detail Trial Balance",FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text008),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(USERID,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text009),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(TODAY,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn(FORMAT(Text010),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddInfoColumn("G/L Account".GETFILTERS,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,FALSE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.ClearNewRow;
      IF Printdetails THEN
        MakeExcelDataHeader
      ELSE
        MakeExcelDataHeaderSumary;
    END;

    PROCEDURE MakeExcelDataBody@4(VAR Param_AppliedBy2@1102159001 : Text[1024];VAR Param_AppliedDate2@1102159002 : Text[1024]);
    VAR
      BlankFiller@1000 : Text[250];
      GLSetup@1000000000 : Record 98;
      DimValue@1000000001 : Record 349;
      GlbDim1@1000000002 : Code[100];
      GlbDim2@1000000003 : Code[100];
      SrtCut1@1000000004 : Code[100];
    BEGIN
      //MESSAGE('hello..'+Param_AppliedBy2+Param_AppliedDate2);


      GLSetup.GET;
      //UGP13R2DEV
      //IF ("G/L Entry".CALCFIELDS("G/L Entry"."Selling Exp")) THEN;

      GlbDim1:='';
      GlbDim2:='';
      SrtCut1:='';
      DimValue.RESET;
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code");
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue.Code,"G/L Entry"."Global Dimension 1 Code");
        IF DimValue.FINDFIRST THEN
          GlbDim1:=DimValue.Name;
          Desc :=DimValue.Description;
          //Message(GlbDim1);


      DimValue.RESET;
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue.Code,"G/L Entry"."Global Dimension 2 Code");
        IF DimValue.FINDFIRST THEN
          GlbDim2:=DimValue.Name;

      "G/L Entry".CALCFIELDS("G/L Entry"."Selling Exp");
      DimValue.RESET;
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue."Dimension Code",GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 3 Code");
      DimValue.SETRANGE(DimValue.Code,"G/L Entry"."Selling Exp");
        IF DimValue.FINDFIRST THEN
          SrtCut1:=DimValue.Name;




      ExcelBuf.NewRow;

      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."G/L Account No."),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text); //nk
      IF "G/L Account".GET("G/L Entry"."G/L Account No.") THEN  //NK
        ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Account".Name),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text); //nk


      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Posting Date"),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Slip No."),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Type Of Transaction"),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Document No."),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(Vend_Supp),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."External Document No."),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(PONUM),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(CurrCod),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);





      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(SrtCut1,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(GlbDim2,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(GlbDim1,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);

      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(Desc,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);


      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(Narr),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(DrOrig),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(CrOrig),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Debit Amount"),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT("G/L Entry"."Credit Amount"),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(GLBalance),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);

      //#DB

      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(Param_AppliedBy2),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text); //Settlement slip no
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(Param_AppliedDate2),FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text); //settlement date

      ////YIMMDEVIP1.0

      IF ("G/L Entry"."Reason Code" = 'SALRT') AND ("G/L Entry"."Bank Account No." = '') THEN BEGIN
          ExcelBuf.AddColumn(Bname,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
          ExcelBuf.AddColumn(Bno,FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      END
      ELSE BEGIN
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn("G/L Entry"."Bank Name Cust/Vend",FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn("G/L Entry"."Bank Account No.",FALSE,'',FALSE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      END;

      Bname :='';
      Bno:='';
      //YIMMDEVIP1.0
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateExcelbook@1102159001();

      ERROR('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE MakePageCounterBody2@1102159031();
    BEGIN

      IF PrintToExcel THEN
      IF NOT Printdetails THEN
      BEGIN
      //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
      //Message(format("G/L Account"."No.")+'   '+format("G/L Account".Name));
      ExcelBuf.NewRow;
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn("G/L Account"."No.",FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn("G/L Account".Name,FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Text);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number); //NK
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number); //NK

      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('Opening Balance',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(StartBalance,FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);

      { //NK.begin
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);


      IF (StartBalance>0) THEN
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(ABS(StartBalance)),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number)
      ELSE
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);

      IF (StartBalance<0) THEN
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn(FORMAT(ABS(StartBalance)),FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number)
      ELSE
      ExcelBuf.AddColumn('',FALSE,'',TRUE,FALSE,TRUE,'',ExcelBuf."Cell Type"::Number);
      } //NK.end
      END;

      //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(NOT (Printdetails));


      //IF PrintToExcel THEN
      //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GLEntry_GF4@1102159009();
    BEGIN

      CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT:=
        CurrReport.TOTALSCAUSEDBY="G/L Entry".FIELDNO("G/L Entry"."Source No.");

      SourceStartBal:= 0;
      IF GLDateFilter <> '' THEN
        IF "G/L Account".GETRANGEMIN("G/L Account"."Date Filter") <> 0D THEN BEGIN
          GlEntryRec.RESET;
          GlEntryRec.SETCURRENTKEY("Source Type","Source No.","G/L Account No.","Posting Date");
          GlEntryRec.SETRANGE(GlEntryRec."Source Type","G/L Entry"."Source Type");
          GlEntryRec.SETRANGE(GlEntryRec."Source No.","G/L Entry"."Source No.");
          GlEntryRec.SETRANGE(GlEntryRec."G/L Account No.","G/L Entry"."G/L Account No.");
          GlEntryRec.SETRANGE(GlEntryRec."Posting Date",0D,CLOSINGDATE("G/L Account".GETRANGEMIN("G/L Account"."Date Filter") - 1));
          IF GlEntryRec.FIND('-')  THEN
            REPEAT
            SourceStartBal += GlEntryRec.Amount;
            UNTIL GlEntryRec.NEXT=0;
        END;

      //IF CurrReport.TOTALSCAUSEDBY="G/L Entry".FIELDNO("G/L Entry"."Source No.") THEN
        //BEGIN
        //Message('hello...');
          AccTotSourceStartBal +=SourceStartBal;
        AccBalance+=GLEntryAmt;
        //Message('gf '+format(AccBalance)+'  '+format(GLEntryAmt));
        //END;


      IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
      //IF   CurrReport.TOTALSCAUSEDBY="G/L Entry".FIELDNO("G/L Entry"."Source No.") THEN
      IF NOT Printdetails THEN
      BEGIN
      //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);

      GLEntryGroupFooter4:=FALSE;
      MakeExcelDataGroupFooter;
      END;
      END;

        IF Printdetails THEN BEGIN
         // CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
      GLEntryGroupFooter4:=FALSE;
      END;


        //  MESSAGE(FORMAT(AccBalance));
      //Message(Format(SourceStartBal)+'    '+Format(DrAmtLcy));
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindApplnEntriesDtldtLedgEntry@1102159003();
    VAR
      DtldCustLedgEntry1@1001 : Record 379;
      DtldCustLedgEntry2@1000 : Record 379;
    BEGIN

      //YIMMDEVIP1.0 start

      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETCURRENTKEY("Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETRANGE("Cust. Ledger Entry No.",CreateCustLedgEntry."Entry No.");
      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETRANGE(Unapplied,FALSE);
      IF DtldCustLedgEntry1.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF DtldCustLedgEntry1."Cust. Ledger Entry No." =
             DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No."
          THEN BEGIN
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.INIT;
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETCURRENTKEY("Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.","Entry Type");
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE(
              "Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE("Entry Type",DtldCustLedgEntry2."Entry Type"::Application);
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE(Unapplied,FALSE);
            IF DtldCustLedgEntry2.FIND('-') THEN
              REPEAT
                IF DtldCustLedgEntry2."Cust. Ledger Entry No." <>
                   DtldCustLedgEntry2."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No."
                THEN BEGIN
                  cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
                  cle.SETRANGE("Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry2."Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
                  IF cle.FIND('-') THEN
                    cle.MARK(TRUE);
                END;
              UNTIL DtldCustLedgEntry2.NEXT = 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
            cle.SETRANGE("Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
            IF cle.FIND('-') THEN
              cle.MARK(TRUE);
          END;
        UNTIL DtldCustLedgEntry1.NEXT = 0;
      //YIMMDEVIP1.0  end
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckAppliedBy@1102159002(VAR RecLoc@1102159001 : Record 21);
    VAR
      CLE_LOC@1102159002 : Record 21;
    BEGIN
      {
      //YIMMDEVIP1.0 start

      //UPG13R2DEV.begin
      //deepa
      CLE_LOC.RESET;
      //CLE_LOC := RecLoc;
      //CLE_LOC.COPYFILTERS(RecLoc);
      CLE_LOC.SETRANGE("Document No.","G/L Entry"."Document No.");
      CLE_LOC.
      CLE_LOC.SETFILTER("Slip No.",'<>%1','');

      IF(CLE_LOC.FINDSET) THEN
      REPEAT
      //IF STRLEN(AppliedBy) < 1000 THEN //NK
        AppliedBy := CLE_LOC."Slip No."+'|'+AppliedBy;
      //  message(AppliedBy);
      //Message(Format(cle."Slip Date")+' '+format(cle."Slip No."));
      //IF(cle."Slip Date"<>0D)     THEN
      AppliedDate := AppliedDate + '|' + FORMAT(CLE_LOC."Slip Date");
      UNTIL CLE_LOC.NEXT = 0;

      IF((AppliedBy<>'') OR(AppliedDate<>'')) THEN BEGIN
      AppliedBy:= DELSTR(AppliedBy,STRLEN(AppliedBy),1);
      AppliedDate:= DELSTR(AppliedDate,STRLEN(AppliedDate),1);
      END;

      //AppliedBy := COPYSTR(AppliedBy,1,1023);
      //UPG13R2DEV.end

      }
      {
      cle.RESET;
      AppliedBy := '';
      AppliedDate := '';
      cle := RecLoc;
      IF cle."Entry No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        CreateCustLedgEntry := cle;
        FindApplnEntriesDtldtLedgEntry;
        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Entry No.");

        IF CreateCustLedgEntry."Closed by Entry No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          cle."Entry No." := CreateCustLedgEntry."Closed by Entry No.";
          cle.MARK(TRUE);
        END;

        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Closed by Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Closed by Entry No.",CreateCustLedgEntry."Entry No.");
        IF cle.FIND('-') THEN
          REPEAT
            cle.MARK(TRUE);
          UNTIL RecLoc.NEXT = 0;

        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Closed by Entry No.");
      END;

      cle.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);


      IF cle.FINDFIRST THEN
      BEGIN
        AppliedBy :=cle."Slip No.";
        MESSAGE(AppliedBy);
        AppliedDate := FORMAT(cle."Slip Date");
      END;
      IF cle.NEXT <> 0 THEN
      }






      cle.RESET;
      AppliedBy := '';
      AppliedDate := '';
      cle := RecLoc;
      IF cle."Entry No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        CreateCustLedgEntry := cle;
        FindApplnEntriesDtldtLedgEntry;
        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Entry No.");

        IF CreateCustLedgEntry."Closed by Entry No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          cle."Entry No." := CreateCustLedgEntry."Closed by Entry No.";
          cle.MARK(TRUE);
        END;

        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Closed by Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Closed by Entry No.",CreateCustLedgEntry."Entry No.");
        IF cle.FIND('-') THEN
          REPEAT
            cle.MARK(TRUE);
          UNTIL RecLoc.NEXT = 0;

        cle.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
        cle.SETRANGE("Closed by Entry No.");
      END;

      cle.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);

      IF cle.FINDFIRST THEN
      BEGIN
        AppliedBy :=cle."Slip No.";
        //MESSAGE(AppliedBy);
        AppliedDate := FORMAT(cle."Slip Date");
      END;
      IF cle.NEXT <> 0 THEN
      REPEAT
        //AppliedBy := AppliedBy+'|'+cle."Slip No.";
        //AppliedDate := AppliedDate + '|' + FORMAT(cle."Slip Date");
      UNTIL cle.NEXT = 0;




      //YIMMDEVIP1.0 end
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetLine@1000000011(GLCode@1000000000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      GLELOC@1000000001 : Record 17;
    BEGIN
      IF GLDateFilter <> '' THEN BEGIN
        GLELOC.SETFILTER("Posting Date",GLDateFilter);
        GLELOC.SETRANGE("G/L Account No.",GLCode);
        IF NOT GLELOC.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          MakePageCounterBody1;
          MakePageCounterBody11;
          MakePageCounterBody2;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
       //UPG13R2DEV
       //I HAVE DELETED ALL GROUPINGS FROM ORIGINAL REPORT AND CREATE NEW ONE and also done some changes in Group footer code.

       //To show settlement slip no,settlement date,bank a/c no,bank a/c name ,both print to excel and printdetails must be checked.

      //YIMMDEVIP1.0

        Point no  -

         33         I have included following fields in excel only:
                    Settlement slip no.
                    Date of settlement
                    Bank Account No.
                    Bank Account Name


         31        showing account number & account name in each line against each record in excel only
    }
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function



Shared RunningTotals As New System.Collections.Hashtable

Public Function GetRunningTotal(ByVal CurrentPageNumber)

Return IIF(CurrentPageNumber &gt; 0, RunningTotals(CurrentPageNumber), 0)

End Function

 

Public Function SetRunningTotal(ByVal CurrentPageTotal, ByVal CurrentPageNumber)

RunningTotals(CurrentPageNumber) = CurrentPageTotal + GetRunningTotal(CurrentPageNumber - 1)

Return RunningTotals(CurrentPageNumber)

End Function 




Private running As Double = 0
Public Function SetTotal(ByVal val As Double) As Double 
    running = val 
    Return val 
End Function
Public Function GetTotal() As Double 
    Return running 
End Function
Private Header As Boolean = 0
Public Function SetShowHeader(ByVal val As Boolean) As Boolean 
    Header = val 
    Return val 
End Function
Public Function GetShowHeader() As Boolean 
    Return Header 
End Function
